–ø—Ä–∏–º–µ—Ä —Å –º–æ–¥–µ–ª—å—é –≤—ã—à–µ, –Ω–∞ $mol –ø—Ä–∏–º–µ—Ä–Ω–æ —Ç–∞–∫ –±—É–¥–µ—Ç –≤—ã–≥–ª—è–¥–∏—Ç—å:

type Person = { name: string, age: number }
class App extends $mol_list {
    
    @ $mol_mem
    persons(next?: Person[]) {
        return next ?? [{ name: 'Alex', age: 19 }, {.name: 'Piter', age: 25 }, { name: 'Alice', age: 35 }]
    }

    @ $mol_mem_key
    Person(item: Person) {
        const obj = new $mol_view
        obj.sub = () => [this.person_name(item)]
        return obj
    }

    person_name(obj: Person) {
        return obj.name
    }

    @ $mol_mem
    rows() {
        return this.persons()
            .filter(obj => obj.age < 30)
            .map(obj => this.Person(obj)
    }

    @ $mol_action
    person(index: number, next?: Person) {
        const list = this.persons()

        if (next === undefined) return list[index]

        this.persons([
            ... list.slice(0, index),
            next,
            ... list.slice(index + 1),
        ])

        return next
    }
}
